### Army Tree ###

shared_focus = {
	id = TRD_decentralised_command
	icon = GFX_goal_secret_agents
	cost = 8.00
	available = {
		has_country_flag = TRD_something_has_happened
        hidden_trigger = { 
		    OR = {
		        NOT = {
			        has_completed_focus = TRD_absolute_power
					has_country_flag = TRD_council_blowback
			    }
			}
        }		
	}
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = TRD_centralised_command }
	ai_will_do = { factor = 90 }
	x = -15
	y = 0
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TRD_decentralised_command"
		army_experience = 25
		add_ideas = TRD_decentralised_command_idea
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = TRD_motor_factories
	icon = GFX_goal_SOV_tractors
	x = -3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = TRD_decentralised_command
	cost = 8.00
	prerequisite = { focus = TRD_decentralised_command }
	available = {
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
			free_building_slots = {
				building = arms_factory
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 90
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TRD_motor_factories"
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
		show_ideas_tooltip = orthos
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
		show_ideas_tooltip = elsevier
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
		show_ideas_tooltip = fugro
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_tech = superior_firepower

				is_researching_technology = mass_assault

				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = TRD_actual_draft
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_strike_at_democracy1
	x = -1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = TRD_red_army
	cost = 8.00
	prerequisite = { focus = TRD_red_army }

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 90
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TRD_actual_draft"
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = disarmed_nation }
			add_ideas = volunteer_only
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = volunteer_only }
			add_ideas = limited_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = limited_conscription }
			add_ideas = extensive_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = extensive_conscription }
			add_ideas = service_by_requirement
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = service_by_requirement }
			add_ideas = all_adults_serve
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = all_adults_serve }
			add_ideas = scraping_the_barrel
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = TRD_empire_rising
	icon = GFX_goal_DOM_The_Phoenix
	x = 0
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = TRD_reclaim_the_birthright
	cost = 8.00
	prerequisite = { focus = TRD_take_feathisia_griefenmarschen }
	prerequisite = { focus = TRD_take_strawberry_bronzehill }
	prerequisite = { focus = TRD_take_yale_romau }
	prerequisite = { focus = TRD_katerin_angriver }
	available = {
	    has_government = fascism
	}
	bypass = { 
	    custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = GRI_core_FAT_SRS_MNC_VED_HAU_tp
		    FAT = {
			    OR = {
				    exists = no
				    is_subject_of = ROOT
			    }
		    }
			SRS = {
			    OR = {
				    exists = no
				    is_subject_of = ROOT
			    }
		    }
			MNC = {
			    OR = {
				    exists = no
				    is_subject_of = ROOT
			    }
		    }
			VED = {
			    OR = {
				    exists = no
				    is_subject_of = ROOT
			    }
		    }
			HAU = {
			    OR = {
				    exists = no
				    is_subject_of = ROOT
			    }
		    }
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 200
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TRD_empire_rising"
		custom_effect_tooltip = ANG_heartland_cores_tp
		add_ideas = GRI_rising_empire
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = BRZ
						is_core_of = KAT 
						is_core_of = STW 
						is_core_of = FEA 
						is_core_of = YAL 
						is_core_of = ANG 
						is_core_of = ROU
						is_core_of = PYT
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}

			if = {
				limit = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = FEA transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = BRZ transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = KAT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ROU transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = YAL transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { PYT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PYT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = STW transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			news_event = { id = tradefed_news.1 hours = 6 } 
			set_global_flag = GRI_empire_rising_flag
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = TRD_strike_north
	icon = GFX_goal_purge_opposition
	x = -4
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = TRD_empire_rising
	cost = 8.00
	prerequisite = { focus = TRD_empire_rising }
	available = {
	    has_government = fascism
		is_subject = no
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 160
		modifier = {
			has_war = yes
			factor = 0.1
		}
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = FAT
	will_lead_to_war_with = FAW
	will_lead_to_war_with = SRS
	will_lead_to_war_with = MNC
	will_lead_to_war_with = HAU
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TRD_strike_north"
		effect_tooltip = { create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = FAT } }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = FAT
				ROOT = { create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
			    country_exists = FAW 
			}
			create_wargoal = { 
			    type = annex_everything 
			    target = FAW 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
			    country_exists = HAU 
			}
			create_wargoal = { 
			    type = annex_everything 
			    target = HAU 
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = SRS }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = SRS
				ROOT = {
					create_wargoal = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
			    MNC = { exists = yes } 
			}
			create_wargoal = { 
			    type = annex_everything 
				target = MNC 
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

				include_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 90
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TRD_arm_the_people"
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = civilian_economy }
			add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation }
			add_ideas = partial_economic_mobilisation
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation }
			add_ideas = war_economy
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = war_economy }
			add_ideas = tot_economic_mobilisation
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
